   22 : savemesh (Th, "results_case1_non_linear/mesh_initial.msh" );
   23 : while(stopmesh > tolmesh && ii < maxit){
   24 : 
   25 : 	jj = 0;
   26 : 
   27 : 	// Power penalty law
   28 : 	if(pen) q = qmax - 2 * exp(- ii / 2.); //q = 3/maxit * ii + 1;
   29 : 	else q = qmax;
   30 : 
   31 : 
   32 : 	IPOPT(J, gradJ, ipC, ipGradC, v[],

   48 : 			v = vHelm;
   49 : 		}

   60 :   }
   61 : 
   62 : 	// Heaviside filtering
   63 : 	if(heav){

   65 : 		real betaH = 10*(ii < 19) + 7*(ii == 19);
   66 : 		vHeav = 0.5 + tanh(betaH*(v-0.5))/(2*tanh(0.5*betaH));
   67 :     plot(vHeav, wait = 1, fill = 1, value = 1, ps = "results_case1_non_linear/"+ii+"_density_postHeav.ps", cmm = "Density postHeav"+ii);
   68 :     v = vHeav;
   69 : 	}
   70 : 
   71 : 	// Sigmund filtering
   72 : 	if(sig){ /* && ii%2==1*/
   73 : 		if(ii != maxit - 1 ){
   74 : 			// beta = 2. * beta; //se vogliamo raddoppiare beta ad ogni iterazione ii
   75 : 			// beta = betamax - (betamax - betamin) * exp(- ii / 2); //se vogliamo incrementare più "soft"
   76 : 			// eta = (ii <= 2)*0.4 + (ii > 2 && ii <= 4)*0.5 + (ii > 4)*0.55;
   77 : 			plot(v,  wait = 1, fill = 1, value = 1, ps = "results_case1_non_linear/"+ii+"_density_preSig.ps", cmm = "Density preSig"+ii);
   78 : 			vSig = (1-xlb) * (tanh(beta * eta) + tanh(beta * (v - xlb - eta)))
   79 : 		                 / (tanh(beta * eta) + tanh(beta * (1 - xlb - eta))) + xlb;
   80 : 			plot(vSig, wait = 1, fill = 1, value = 1, ps = "results_case1_non_linear/"+ii+"_density_postSig.ps", cmm = "Density postSig"+ii);
   81 : 			v = vSig;
   82 : 			//beta += 1;
   83 : 			beta = beta * 2.;
   84 : 			//eta += 0.02;
   85 : 		}
   86 : 	}
   87 : 
   88 :   // Mesh projection (only for mesh adaptivity)
   89 :   if(meshad){
   90 :   	v = v;
   91 :   	xlb = xlb;
   92 :   	xub = xub;
   93 :   	gvi = gvi;
   94 :   	gvj = 0:Xhp.ndof-1;
   95 :   	lz = lz;
   96 :   	uz = uz;

   98 :   	m12 = m12;
   99 :   	m22 = m22;
  100 : 
  101 :   	stopmesh = abs(Th.nt - real(ntold))/ntold;
  102 :   }
  103 : 
  104 : 	ii += 1;
  105 : 
  106 : 	cout << "Iteration " << ii << ", Mesh error = " << stopmesh << endl;
  107 : 
  108 : 	{
  109 : 	ofstream fout("results_case1_non_linear/"+ii+"_density.txt");
  110 : 	fout << v[];
  111 : 	}
  112 : 	plot(v,  wait = 1, fill = 1, value = 1, ps = "results_case1_non_linear/"+ii+"_density.ps", cmm = "Density "+ii);

  118 : cout << Th.nt << endl;
